> **Stamp**: 2026-05-15 (rev 110) — **Sprint F-4.3 ✅ DONE — Plugin Review System fully wired**. **Deliverables (5 items)**: **(1) `server/dbMigrate.js` (EXTENDED)** — `plugin_reviews` table added (section 15b): `id` UUID PK, `plugin_id` TEXT, `user_id` TEXT, `reviewer_label` TEXT (masked email stored at write time), `rating` INTEGER with `CHECK (rating >= 1 AND rating <= 5)`, `body` TEXT (max 2000), `created_at`/`updated_at` TIMESTAMPTZ, `UNIQUE(user_id, plugin_id)`, two covering indexes. Table is created idempotently via `CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS`. **(2) `server.js` (EXTENDED — 2 endpoints)** — `maskEmail()` helper (shows `ab***@domain.com`); `GET /marketplace/api/plugins/:id(*)/reviews` — public endpoint, optional Bearer token resolves caller for `isOwn` flag, parallel queries for paginated list + aggregate (AVG/COUNT), falls back to empty list if DB unavailable; `POST /marketplace/api/plugins/:id(*)/reviews` — auth-required, validates `rating` (1-5) and `body` (≤2000), upserts via `ON CONFLICT (user_id, plugin_id) DO UPDATE`, returns full review shape with `isOwn: true`. **(3) `apps/marketplace/src/api/client.ts` (EXTENDED)** — `PluginReview` and `ReviewListResult` interfaces added; `listReviews(pluginId, token?)` and `submitReview(pluginId, { rating, body? > **Stamp**: 2026-05-15 (rev 106) — **rAF gate regression ✅ FIXED — `check-raf-count` exits 0; 1 owner; build ✅**. **Regression**: `check-raf-count.ts` (HARD_FAIL=1) was exiting 1 because `apps/editor/src/engine/initScene.ts` contained a raw `requestAnimationFrame(` call (lines 850–857) introduced in Sprint F-P2 (ResizeObserver container size fix). The gate's `| wc -l` pipe caused the exit code to be captured as `tail`'s exit code in prior multi-gate runs, masking the failure. **Root cause**: The F-P2 fix (2026-05-15) wired a `ResizeObserver` coalescer using the raw rAF pattern (`let resizeRafId | requestAnimationFrame(() => { ... })`) instead of the canonical `getFrameScheduler().scheduleOnce()` — violating §P3 (single-rAF-owner rule) and the Wave 7 D.7.8 final ratchet (HARD_FAIL=1). **Fix**: Replaced the 7-line `resizeRafId` + `requestAnimationFrame()` coalescer in `initScene.ts` lines 844–860 with `getFrameScheduler().scheduleOnce('initScene-resize-coalesce', () => { resize(); scheduleRPMRebuild(); })`. The named key `'initScene-resize-coalesce'` provides the same deduplication guarantee as the former null-guard without a captured handle. `getFrameScheduler` was already imported at line 42. **Gate result**: `rg -l 'requestAnimationFrame\(' . --type ts [exclusions] | wc -l` → 1 (only `packages/frame-scheduler/src/RafAdapter.ts`). `check-raf-count.ts` → `[raf-tripwire] OK: 1 owner.` EXIT:0 ✅. `npm run build` → EXIT:0 (vite 1m 3s) ✅. **Files changed**: `apps/editor/src/engine/initScene.ts` (7 lines → 4 lines; raw rAF removed).

> **Stamp**: 2026-05-15 (rev 105) — **Sprint F-2.2 ✅ DONE — `getCommandManagerBridge()` typed helper; 25 illegal `(window as any).commandManager` casts collapsed to one auditable site; build ✅ TSC = 0 ✅**. **Problem**: 24 plugin bridge handler files (F-1.3 migration bridges, across `plugins/curtain-wall/`, `plugins/furniture/`, `plugins/levels/`, `plugins/plumbing/`, `plugins/roof/`, `plugins/rooms/`, `plugins/selection/`, `plugins/slab/`, `plugins/stair/`, `plugins/view/`, `plugins/wall/`) each contained a bare `const cm = (window as any).commandManager;` cast — 25 total sites (24 plugin handlers + `packages/room-topology/src/RoomTagAutoPopulator.ts`). Doc 23 §9 prohibits local `(window as any)` casts. The `Window.commandManager` type IS declared in `packages/command-registry/src/global-window-augment.d.ts` but plugins couldn't access it without a proper helper. **Solution**: **(1) `packages/command-registry/src/global-bridge.ts` created** — exports `LegacyCommandManager` interface (`execute(cmd: unknown, options?: unknown): void`) and `getCommandManagerBridge(): LegacyCommandManager | undefined`. Collapses all 25 `(window as any)` casts to one single suppression-free call (`window.commandManager as LegacyCommandManager | undefined`) using the pre-existing Window augmentation in the same package. TODO(F-2.x) comment anchors removal once bridge handlers are fully replaced with Immer store writes. **(2) `packages/command-registry/src/index.ts`** — added `export { getCommandManagerBridge, type LegacyCommandManager } from './global-bridge.js'`. **(3) All 24 plugin bridge handler files updated**: `import { ..., getCommandManagerBridge } from '@pryzm/command-registry'` + `const cm = getCommandManagerBridge();`. `eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any` comment removed from `plugins/view/src/handlers/DeleteElement.ts`. Stale comments "Uses the (window as any).commandManager pattern established by RenameRoomHandler" updated to reference the bridge function. **(4) `packages/room-topology/src/RoomTagAutoPopulator.ts`** — `this._commandManager ?? (window as any).commandManager` → `this._commandManager ?? getCommandManagerBridge()`. **Verification**: `(window as any).commandManager` grep across plugins/packages/apps → 6 results, ALL in comments (JSDoc/line comments) — zero actual code casts remain. `check-no-commandmanager` gate = 0 ✅. `check-cast-count` gate = 0 ✅. `check-project-isolation` ✅. TSC `--skipLibCheck` = 0 errors ✅. `npm run build` → EXIT:0 (vite 57.80s, 2957 modules) ✅. **Files changed**: `packages/command-registry/src/global-bridge.ts` (new), `packages/command-registry/src/index.ts` (1 export line), 24 plugin handler files, `packages/room-topology/src/RoomTagAutoPopulator.ts`.

> **Stamp**: 2026-05-13 (rev 94) — **G2-T1 ✅ DONE — GPU hover pick throttled to 1 pick per rAF frame (`SelectionManager._onHoverGpuPickRaf`)**. **Root cause**: `SelectionManager._onPointerMove` called `this._pickStrategy.pick()` synchronously on every `pointermove` DOM event, with only a 50 ms time-throttle. Each GPU pick costs 95–451 ms (ID-buffer render + GPU-CPU readback), causing LONGTASKs that blocked rAF callbacks, stalled camera updates, and capped navigation FPS at 4–8 fps after a batch. **Fix (G2-T1)**: Added 3 new fields to `SelectionManager` — `_pendingHoverClientX: number`, `_pendingHoverClientY: number`, `_hoverRafId: number | null`. In `_onPointerMove`, the synchronous GPU pick block is replaced with: store the latest clientX/Y and call `requestAnimationFrame(_onHoverGpuPickRaf)` once per frame (guarded by `_hoverRafId !== null`). Multiple `pointermove` events between two rAF beats update the position in-place but do NOT queue additional picks. The new `_onHoverGpuPickRaf()` private method clears `_hoverRafId`, re-checks all guards (enabled / isTransforming / isCameraDragging), rebuilds the pick context from the stored pending position, and calls `_pickStrategy.pick()` exactly once. If GPU hits: overrides the BVH hover result already dispatched by `_onPointerMove` (one-frame correction, imperceptible). If GPU misses or throws: BVH result stands. **Why this eliminates LONGTASKs**: `_onPointerMove` now returns in < 1 ms regardless of scene size. GPU pick LONGTASKs are confined to rAF callbacks (expected place for expensive GPU work). Navigation and camera orbit/pan are no longer blocked by hover picks. **Invariant preserved**: click path pick at line 670 is untouched — click picks are still synchronous and immediate (must be, for accurate click-target selection). **TSC = 0 ✅. Zero breaking changes. Files changed**: `packages/input-host/src/SelectionManager.ts` (3 new fields at lines 114–129, `_onPointerMove` GPU pick block replaced at lines 2293–2306, `_onHoverGpuPickRaf()` method added at lines 2337–2392).

> **Stamp**: 2026-05-13 (rev 93) — **Priority 1 Geometry Memory Leak Fix ✅ DONE — G1-T1, G1-T2, G1-T3 complete — `50-PLAN-FORWARD-GAP-ANALYSIS.md` published**. **Document (50)**: Comprehensive 10-gap registry written for `04-PLAN-FORWARD/`. Covers G1 (geometry leak), G2 (post-batch navigation perf), G3 (CRDT blackout), G4 (commandManager.execute() stale sites), G5 (post-AU roadmap missing), G6 (convergence boolean #1 stale), G7 (ghost-file audit needed), G8 (Phase F execution checklist missing), G9 (open-items stale), G10 (command-registry mixed import pattern). Each gap has full evidence, root-cause taxonomy, sprint task board, and acceptance criteria. **Code fix (G1-T1)**: In `packages/core-app-model/src/geometry/NativeElementMeshExporter.ts`, mark ALL IM-derived and Mesh-derived proxy geometries as `sharedGeometry: true` on `geometry.userData` before proxy construction. This ensures `releaseGroups({ disposeProxies: true })` correctly skips disposal of InstancedMesh and source-Mesh geometries that are owned by builders and shared with the live THREE.js scene (disposing them would corrupt 3D scene rendering). **Code fix (G1-T2)**: Removed redundant `group.clear()` loop from `EdgeProjectorService.ts` lines 1963–1966. This loop ran BEFORE the caller's `releaseGroups()`, leaving `group.children` empty by the time `disposeProxies` tried to iterate them — silently defeating the disposal pass. Callers now own full lifecycle cleanup. **Code fix (G1-T3)**: Changed all 8 `nativeElementMeshExporter.releaseGroups(nativeGroups)` call sites to `releaseGroups(nativeGroups, { disposeProxies: true })` across `PlanViewManager.ts` (3 sites: lines 672, 680, 695 + 780 + 795), `ViewController.ts` (5 sites: 435, 454, 1411, 1426, 1536, 1553), `initScene.ts` (1 site: 732). **Why this is safe**: all proxy geometries are now marked `sharedGeometry: true` → `_disposeProxyGroup` skips them → only genuinely new (non-shared) proxy geometries would be disposed (currently zero such proxies exist, but the path is correct for future use). **Why this closes the leak**: the dispose infrastructure is now fully wired; the `RenderPerformanceService` geometry ceiling monitor (`renderer.info.memory.geometries < 12,000`) will no longer false-trigger once the remaining Source B (gpu-pick throttle — G2-T1) and Source C (EPS try/finally — G1-T6) fixes are applied. **TSC=0 ✅. Zero breaking changes.** **Next**: G2 (navigation performance — gpu-pick throttle is the single highest-leverage fix).

> **Stamp**: 2026-05-09 (rev 40) — **Phase 6 Task 6.3 ✅ COMPLETE — Ed25519 plugin signing enforcement (C07 §3)**. **DB**: Added 3 missing tables to `server/dbMigrate.js`: `marketplace_plugins` (was referenced in routes but had no CREATE TABLE — bug fixed; 21 columns including `bundle_url`, `bundle_sha256`, `signature_json`), `plugin_publisher_keys` (Ed25519 public key registry per developer account), `plugin_revocations` (CRL backing store). **`server/pluginSigningService.js` (NEW)**: Pure Node.js Ed25519 verification — `verifyPluginSignatureNode()` (wraps `node:crypto verify()` with SPKI DER header for raw 32-byte keys; mirrors canonical-JSON logic from `packages/plugin-sdk/src/signing.ts`), `lookupPublisherKey()`, `fetchRevocationList()`. **`server.js`** — 4 new routes + 1 enhanced route: (1) `POST /marketplace/api/plugins/submit` enhanced — rejects unsigned plugins (400 MISSING_SIGNATURE), rejects unregistered public keys (403 UNREGISTERED_KEY), cryptographically verifies Ed25519 signature (403 SIGNATURE_VERIFICATION_FAILED), stores `signature_json` in DB on success; (2) `POST /marketplace/api/publishers/register-key` — register Ed25519 public key (auth; validates 32-byte length); (3) `GET /marketplace/api/publishers/keys` — list keys (auth); (4) `POST /marketplace/api/plugins/:id/install` — re-verify at install time per C07 §4.2; reference plugins pre-verified; third-party rejected if no signature on record; (5) `GET /marketplace/api/revocations.json` — CRL endpoint (public; 1-hour cache header). **`apps/marketplace/src/api/client.ts`** — Full rework: typed interfaces (`MarketplacePlugin`, `PluginSignature`, `InstallPluginResult`, `RevocationList`, `PublisherKey`), new methods `registerPublisherKey`, `listPublisherKeys`, `submitPlugin`, `installPlugin`, `getRevocations`; `MARKETPLACE_BASE` corrected from `/v1` to `/marketplace/api`. **Verifications**: `GET /marketplace/api/revocations.json` → valid CRL JSON ✅; `GET /marketplace/api/plugins` → 5 plugins ✅; all 4 auth-gated routes → 401 without token ✅; `pnpm tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors ✅; server starts cleanly ✅. **C07 §3 acceptance criteria met**: unsigned plugin → 403 MISSING_SIGNATURE; signature-mismatch → 403 SIGNATURE_VERIFICATION_FAILED; CRL endpoint live. **GA gates**: all 11 green ✅. **Files changed**: `server/dbMigrate.js` (+3 tables: marketplace_plugins, plugin_publisher_keys, plugin_revocations), `server/pluginSigningService.js` (NEW — 155 LOC), `server.js` (+4 new routes + enhanced submit), `apps/marketplace/src/api/client.ts` (rewritten with typed interfaces), `docs/03_PRYZM3/04-PLAN-FORWARD/46-IMPLEMENTATION-PLAN-2026-05-08.md` (Task 6.3 → DONE).

> **Stamp**: 2026-05-15 (rev 29) — **Sprint 5 E.3 ✅ COMPLETE — CW_LEVEL_Y_MISMATCH semantic CRDT conflict detection**: `_detectCwLevelYMismatch()` private method added to `YjsDocAdapter` (packages/sync-client/src/YjsDocAdapter.ts). Called from `applyUpdate()` after every `Y.applyUpdate()` merge. Algorithm: (1) build `Map<levelId, levelY>` from known level-command namespaces (`level.update`, `levels.update`, `level.create`) — exits early if no level data (fast-path O(1) for non-level updates); (2) scan CW namespaces (`curtain-wall.create-on-all-slabs`, `curtain-wall.create`, `curtain-wall.batch.create`) for elements with `levelId` referencing a tracked level; (3) compare stored `computedBaseY`/`baseY`/`elevation` vs. level `y`/`elevation`/`baseElevation` — emit `CRDTConflict{ elementId, property:'CW_LEVEL_Y_MISMATCH', localValue:cwBaseY, remoteValue:levelY }` for any |delta| > 1mm. Non-fatal: fully wrapped in try/catch; scan failure is logged and swallowed (never blocks `applyUpdate()`). `§E3-CW_LEVEL_Y_MISMATCH` marker in warn log. **Process tracker audit** (comprehensive ground-truth verification of all Sprint 2–4 tasks — tracker was severely out of date vs. actual source): §10.1 Phase Rollup updated: F ✅ DONE (3/3), G ✅ DONE (3/3), H ✅ DONE (2/2), I ✅ DONE (2/2), K ✅ DONE (2/2), C ✅ DONE (6/6), D ✅ DONE (5/5), E ⚠️ PARTIAL 2/3 (E.2 ⛔ BLOCKED — server seqNo absent). §10.2 Sprint 1 rows: F.1/F.2/F.3 → ✅ DONE. §10.3 Sprint 2: G.1/G.2/G.3/I.1/I.2 → ✅ DONE. §10.4 Sprint 3: H.1/H.2/K.1/K.2 → ✅ DONE. §10.5 Sprint 4: C.2/C.5/C.6/D.4/E.1 → ✅ DONE; E.2 → ⛔ BLOCKED; E.3 → ✅ DONE. doc 45 updates: Phase E rollup 1/3 → 2/3; E.3 task row → ✅ DONE; E.3 spec section status → ✅ DONE; E.3 maintenance table → ✅ DONE. **Gate**: `pnpm run build` → EXIT:0 ✅ (2956 modules, check-project-isolation + tsc --skipLibCheck + vite build + write-prod-shim — all clean). **Files changed**: `packages/sync-client/src/YjsDocAdapter.ts` (E.3 `_detectCwLevelYMismatch` + `applyUpdate` hook, ~85 LOC added), `docs/03_PRYZM3/04-PLAN-FORWARD/45-CW-SLAB-BATCH-IMPLEMENTATION-PLAN.md` (E.3 task row + spec status + Phase E rollup + maintenance table), `docs/03_PRYZM3/00-PROCESS-TRACKER.md` (§10.1–§10.5 all rows corrected).

> **Stamp**: 2026-05-04 (rev 24) — **Sprint A38 — §PERF-VIEW-BATCH-SUPPRESS + §PERF-3D-SKIP + §BATCH-INDICATOR-RAF (runtime performance fixes)**: Two live runtime performance regressions diagnosed and fixed. (1) **§PERF-VIEW-BATCH-SUPPRESS** — `ViewDependencyTracker._onStoreEvent` was firing on every one of the 3,960–6,072 store events delivered during `endBatchYielded()` drain, continuously resetting the 300ms debounce timer; after drain the `elementId-not-registered` fallback path marked ALL views dirty (including `viewType='3d'`), causing EdgeProjectorService to project 9,461 edge geometries for the 3D system view → **12,635ms LONGTASK**. Fix: added `_batchSuppressed` flag + `setSuppressed(bool)` + `markLevelsDirty(levelIds[])` public methods on `ViewDependencyTracker`; added early-return guard in `_onStoreEvent` when `_batchSuppressed`; excluded `viewType === '3d'` from both `_getAffectedViews()` and the fallback (all-views) path. `BatchCoordinator._setupBatch()` now calls `setSuppressed(true)`; `onComplete()` calls `setSuppressed(false)` + `markLevelsDirty(levelIds)` after `_isBatching=false`; `forceReset()` calls `setSuppressed(false)`. **Result**: 3D system view excluded from all projections; 9,461 → 561 edge geometries projected (94% reduction, 1 plan view only); no debounce avalanche after drain. (2) **§PERF-3D-SKIP** — defense-in-depth guard `if (viewDef.viewType === '3d') return;` added at top of `onReprojectionNeeded` callback in `initScene.ts`. (3) **§BATCH-INDICATOR-RAF** — `BatchLoadingIndicator._animateBar()` was using raw `requestAnimationFrame` (violating §P3 single-rAF-owner rule and risking indefinite spin if indicator was hidden mid-animation). Fixed: replaced with `getFrameScheduler().addTickListener('pryzm-batch-indicator-bar', tick, 'overlay')`; added `_barAnimDispose` field + `_stopBarAnim()` helper; `hide()` calls `_stopBarAnim()` first. **Files changed**: `ViewDependencyTracker.ts` (367→374 lines, 4 new public/private members), `BatchCoordinator.ts` (880→903 lines, suppression calls in `_setupBatch`/`onComplete`/`forceReset`), `initScene.ts` (2263 lines, 1 guard), `BatchLoadingIndicator.ts` (424→451 lines, FrameScheduler bar anim). **GA gates**: `tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors ✅; live batch test → 1 plan view flushed (3D excluded) ✅; 561 edge geometries projected (was 9,461) ✅; no LONGTASK avalanche post-drain ✅.

Target ≤10 ms/frame. Resets to 5 at builder construction. Debug log shows `nextBudget=N`. (2) **§PERF-BATCH-BUS** — `CreateCurtainWallsOnAllSlabsCommand` bus dispatch block (lines 260–303) re-ran the full polygon/winding-order/edge-loop over all slabs a second time to reconstruct `busCwSpecs`. Wired in `engineLauncher.ts` after `batchCoordinator.inject()`. TSC 0 errors ✅. **GA gates**: adaptive-drain code present ✅; batch-indicator visible ✅; `pnpm tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors ✅.

> **Stamp**: 2026-05-04 (rev 22) — **Wave 35 Deep Audit — D1 critical defect found and fixed**: Deep architectural audit of all Wave 35 implementation files revealed one critical defect (D1) and two pre-existing minor gaps. D1: `forceReset()` did not call `storeEventBus.endBatch()` (or equivalent) when `_isBatching=true`. If a batch was mid-flight at the moment `pryzm-project-switch` fired, `storeEventBus._batchDepth` remained at 1 permanently — every subsequent Project B store event would be buffered indefinitely and never flushed to builders → builders receive no creates → scene stays empty for the entire Project B session. Fix: (1) `StoreEventBus.discardBatch()` added to `@pryzm/core-app-model` — atomically resets `_batchDepth=0` and `_buffer=[]` WITHOUT flushing stale Project A events to listeners and WITHOUT touching listener subscriptions (contrast with `clear()` which removes listeners). (2) `BatchCoordinator.forceReset()` step 3 added: `if (this._isBatching) { storeEventBus.discardBatch(); }` — closes the outer bracket cleanly before clearing state. Minor gaps (pre-existing, not Wave 35 regressions): G1 = dynamic import path in `_executeFinalSweep()` has a narrow race window (import resolves after `_sweepCancelled=false` microtask); G2 = `resumeAndFlush()` on CW/Slab in teardown steps 3-4 may build ~1 frame of zombie Project A geometry before store clearing — acceptable. Architecture verdict: Sound with D1 fix applied. **GA gates (9/9)**: cast-count=15 ✅; raf-count=1 ✅; ctrl-z-wired ✅; otel-spans=183/183 ✅; l7-boundary=ratchet-holding ✅; project-isolation=4/4 ✅; `pnpm tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors ✅.

> **Authority**: This section is the executive-layer strategic assessment. Full evidence, gap analysis, and competitor breakdown live in `05-ARCHITECTURE-BREAKDOWN.md §11`. This section is the one-stop tracker summary: current score, competitor position, the 20 gaps, and the verdict. Update whenever the overall audit score advances.

### §SR.2 — Where PRYZM Stands vs. Each Competitor

| Competitor | PRYZM advantage | PRYZM gap |
|---|---|---|
| **Autodesk Revit** | Browser-native (no installer), open IFC (not RVT), real-time collab, AI layer, plugin marketplace | Family editor depth, structural analysis, MEP routing, performance at 500k+ Revit elements, documentation sheet completeness |
| **Autodesk Forma** | Open format + authoring (Forma has no BIM authoring), plugin SDK (Forma SDK is read-heavy), 46 element families, BCF, ISO 19650 CDE, offline path-tracer | Geospatial precision (Forma 8/10 vs PRYZM 4/10), urban zoning tools, environmental analysis integration |
| **Pascal BIM** | Plugin SDK + marketplace model (Pascal has none), AI layer (Pascal has none), real-time collab depth, ISO 19650 state machine | Pascal parametric family editor quality — Pascal's constraint graph and formula editor are more mature than PRYZM's `apps/component-editor/` scaffold |
| **Qonic** | Plugin SDK (Qonic has none), AI layer (Qonic has none), dual render pipeline, ISO 19650, AI-driven design rules | Qonic's IFC-native authoring and geospatial coordinate precision are currently stronger; Qonic has real CRDT vs PRYZM's LWW |
| **IFC.js / Bonsai** | Full BIM authoring (Bonsai is viewer-only), AI layer, plugin marketplace, collaboration | Bonsai's IFC parsing is more fully worker-threaded and buildingSMART-aligned |

**Net position**: PRYZM is the only browser BIM tool with all five: browser-native + open IFC + real-time collab + plugin SDK + AI. No single competitor has all five. The moat is architecturally established; it is not yet commercially capitalized because the score is 5.8/10 and 20 critical gaps remain open.

### §SR.5 — Strategic Verdict

**Yes, PRYZM is on the right path. The architecture is correct. The plan is correct.**

The L0–L9 layer model, single composition root, plugin iframe sandbox, IFC-first data model, and command-bus event sourcing are verified properties of the actual codebase enforced by machine-checkable rules. No competitor is building with comparable structural discipline.

**Three non-negotiable prerequisites before any enterprise pitch:**

1. **Wave A14 first** — CI gate must block regressions on every PR. Without it, every subsequent wave risks undoing prior work silently.
2. **Wave A19 before any concurrent-editing claim** — LWW silently corrupts models. Do not demo "real-time collaboration" to enterprise prospects until Yjs lands.
3. **Wave A18 before any UK/EU enterprise sales conversation** — accessibility 2/10 is a legal blocker under the Equality Act 2010 and EN 301 549.

**Execution order is non-negotiable: A14 → A15 → A16 → A17 → A18 → A19 → A20 → GA.**

> Full competitive analysis: `05-ARCHITECTURE-BREAKDOWN.md §11`. Full wave plans: `04-PLAN-FORWARD/24-WAVE-A14-*.md` through `30-WAVE-A20-*.md`.

# 2. No (window as any) regressions

# 3. No rAF regressions

  | grep -v 'frame-scheduler\|check-raf' | wc -l                         # → 1

> **Authority**: `docs/03_PRYZM3/04-PLAN-FORWARD/45-CW-SLAB-BATCH-IMPLEMENTATION-PLAN.md` (full spec, change plans, acceptance criteria, code snippets).
> **Scope**: `CreateCurtainWallsOnAllSlabsCommand` batch pipeline — Phases A through J.
> **Status date**: 2026-05-07. **Total tasks**: 37. **Done**: 16. **Remaining**: 21.
> **Legend**: ✅ DONE · 🔄 IN PROGRESS · 🔴 PENDING · ⚠️ EXTEND NEEDED · ⛔ BLOCKED · 🗓️ QUARTERLY
> **Founding constraints**: Memory ≤1.5 GB (C10 NFT-16) · Frame budget ≤16.6ms (NFT-4) · Collaboration (C08) · AI cost (C09) · 1M elements (C11 §7)

### §10.7 — Update Protocol

When completing or starting a task, update **both** this file (§10) **and** the corresponding `**Status**:` line in `45-CW-SLAB-BATCH-IMPLEMENTATION-PLAN.md`.

```
Checklist per task transition:
  1. Change Status cell in §10.x task board row (this file)
  2. Change **Status**: line in doc 45 (e.g., 🔴 PENDING → ✅ DONE)
  3. Update Done/Total in §10.1 Phase Rollup + doc 45 Phase Status Dashboard
  4. If phase complete: update Phase Rollup Status column in both files
  5. pnpm run build → EXIT:0  (no TypeScript regressions)
  6. Stamp new date on > Status date: line in both files
```
